| Ḥemmleɣ ad seddqeɣ kra yedrimen yal aseggas. |
| Ḥemmleɣ ad sleɣ i waman swectilen deg terga. |
| ḤemmleƔ aẓawan aklasiki ugar n uẓawan atrar. |
| Ḥemmleɣ iselman ugar n wanect ḥemmleɣ aksum. |
| Ḥemmleɣ Lezzayer mmuten fell-as yegrawliwen. |
| Ḥemmleɣ Lezzayer mmuten fell-as yeqbayliyen. |
| Ḥemmleɣ tizlit-nni ay d-tecna Kylie Minogue. |
| Ḥemmleɣ-kent ugar n wanect ay iyi-tḥemmlemt. |
| Ḥulfaɣ am wakken yemma tbeddel cwiṭ tikli-s. |
| Ḥulfaɣ i tɣawsa la tesmulḥuc deg weɛrur-inu. |
| Ḥwajeɣ kra n tɣawsa iyes ara ldiɣ asenduq-a. |
| Ḥwajeɣ tansa-nnek akken ad ak-d-azneɣ asefk. |
| Ḥwajeɣ tansa-nnem akken ad am-d-azneɣ asefk. |
| I d-yeggran d lxubata |  wid i d-teǧǧa fransa. |
| I nekk i d-uɣeɣ adlis-a |  mačči i tmeṭṭut-iw. |
| I nutenti |  d acu i tent-id-igren di tessirt? |
| I teffɣed-d ɣer da |  ad twalid s timmad-nnek? |
| I teffɣeḍ-d ɣer da |  ad twaliḍ s timmad-nnek? |
| I teffɣed-d ɣer da |  ad twalid s timmad-nnem? |
| I teffɣeḍ-d ɣer da |  ad twaliḍ s timmad-nnem? |
| I tezmert-ik akked d wussan ara yelhun ugar! |
| I wacu umi tebɣid tankult tilemt n yerkasen? |
| Iban kan ad ilint tqellqent armi d ayen kan. |
| Iban kan d aqcic-nni ay yerẓan tazewwut-nni. |
| Iban kan imawlan-nwent umaren yes-went mliḥ. |
| Iban kan kennemti d tinesbaɣurin timeqranin. |
| Iban kan teɛyam |  maca ṛjut arma d tis kraḍt. |
| Iban kan teḥṛes iman-nnes mliḥ deg tezrawin. |
| Iban kan tḥeṛsed iman-nnek mliḥ deg uxeddim. |
| Iban kan tḥeṛsed iman-nnem mliḥ deg uxeddim. |
